```csharp
using UnityEngine;

/// <summary>
/// Defines a building entrance with an inspector-assigned doorway entry point and an interior spawn point.
/// 
/// Scene setup:
/// - Attach this component to the building root.
/// - Assign EntryPoint to a child Transform at the doorway.
/// - Assign InteriorSpawnPoint to a Transform inside the building.
/// - Assign DoorTriggerCollider to a trigger collider at the doorway, or leave it empty and place a trigger collider on EntryPoint.
/// - Ensure the player has a collider and uses the Player tag if tag validation is enabled.
/// </summary>
[DisallowMultipleComponent]
public sealed class Building : MonoBehaviour
{
    [Header("Scene References")]
    [SerializeField, Tooltip("Transform at the doorway used as the building entry point.")]
    private Transform _entryPoint;

    [SerializeField, Tooltip("Transform inside the building where the player will spawn after entering.")]
    private Transform _interiorSpawnPoint;

    [SerializeField, Tooltip("Optional doorway trigger collider. If empty, the script will try to use a Collider on EntryPoint.")]
    private Collider _doorTriggerCollider;

    [Header("Interaction")]
    [SerializeField, Tooltip("If enabled, touching the doorway trigger automatically moves the player to the interior spawn point.")]
    private bool _useAutoEnterTrigger = true;

    [SerializeField, Tooltip("Tag used to validate trigger overlap. Set to empty to disable tag filtering.")]
    private string _playerTag = "Player";

    [SerializeField, Tooltip("Draws gizmos for the entry point and interior spawn point in the Scene view.")]
    private bool _drawGizmos = true;

    public Transform EntryPoint => _entryPoint;
    public Transform InteriorSpawnPoint => _interiorSpawnPoint;
    public Collider DoorTriggerCollider => _doorTriggerCollider;

    private void Reset()
    {
        AutoAssignReferences();
        EnsureTriggerCollider();
    }

    private void Awake()
    {
        AutoAssignReferences();
        EnsureTriggerCollider();
    }

    private void OnValidate()
    {
        AutoAssignReferences();
        EnsureTriggerCollider();
    }

    private void AutoAssignReferences()
    {
        if (_entryPoint == null && transform.childCount > 0)
        {
            _entryPoint = transform.GetChild(0);
        }

        if (_doorTriggerCollider == null && _entryPoint != null)
        {
            _doorTriggerCollider = _entryPoint.GetComponent<Collider>();
        }
    }

    private void EnsureTriggerCollider()
    {
        if (_doorTriggerCollider != null && !_doorTriggerCollider.isTrigger)
        {
            _doorTriggerCollider.isTrigger = true;
        }
    }

    private void OnTriggerEnter(Collider other)
    {
        if (!_useAutoEnterTrigger)
        {
            return;
        }

        if (!IsPlayer(other))
        {
            return;
        }

        TryEnterBuilding(other.transform);
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Manual entry hook for an interaction system.
    /// Call this when the player presses the interact key while facing the doorway.
    /// </summary>
    public void TryEnterBuilding(Transform playerTransform)
    {
        if (playerTransform == null)
        {
            return;
        }

        if (_interiorSpawnPoint == null)
        {
            Debug.LogWarning($"Building '{name}' is missing an InteriorSpawnPoint reference.", this);
            return;
        }

        playerTransform.SetPositionAndRotation(_interiorSpawnPoint.position, _interiorSpawnPoint.rotation);
    }

    public bool HasValidSetup()
    {
        return _entryPoint != null && _interiorSpawnPoint != null;
    }

    public Transform GetInteriorSpawnPoint()
    {
        return _interiorSpawnPoint;
    }

    private bool IsPlayer(Collider other)
    {
        if (other == null)
        {
            return false;
        }

        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(_playerTag))
        {
            return true;
        }

        return other.CompareTag(_playerTag);
    }

    private void OnDrawGizmos()
    {
        if (!_drawGizmos)
        {
            return;
        }

        if (_entryPoint != null)
        {
            Gizmos.color = Color.cyan;
            Gizmos.DrawWireSphere(_entryPoint.position, 0.25f);
            Gizmos.DrawLine(transform.position, _entryPoint.position);
        }

        if (_interiorSpawnPoint != null)
        {
            Gizmos.color = Color.green;
            Gizmos.DrawWireCube(_interiorSpawnPoint.position, Vector3.one * 0.35f);
        }
    }
}

```

Contents of Assets/Scripts/BuildingTransition.cs:
```csharp
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.SceneManagement;

namespace Omnisense
{
    [DisallowMultipleComponent]
    public class BuildingTransition : MonoBehaviour
    {
        [Header("Entry")]
        [SerializeField] private Transform entryPoint;
        [SerializeField] private float interactRadius = 1.2f;
        [SerializeField] private string playerTag = "Player";
        [SerializeField] private KeyCode interactKey = KeyCode.E;

        [Header("Interior")]
        [SerializeField] private bool loadInteriorScene = false;
        [SerializeField] private string interiorSceneName;
        [SerializeField] private GameObject interiorRoot;
        [SerializeField] private Transform interiorSpawnPoint;
        [SerializeField] private bool hideExteriorOnEnter = true;

        [Header("Player Control")]
        [SerializeField] private CharacterController playerCharacterController;
        [SerializeField] private MonoBehaviour[] componentsToDisableDuringTransition;

        private GameObject _cachedPlayer;
        private bool _transitioning;

        private void Reset()
        {
            entryPoint = transform;
        }

        private void Awake()
        {
            if (entryPoint == null)
            {
                entryPoint = transform;
            }
        }

        private void Update()
        {
            if (_transitioning)
            {
                return;
            }

            if (!Input.GetKeyDown(interactKey))
            {
                return;
            }

            var player = FindPlayerInRange();
            if (player == null)
            {
                return;
            }

            EnterBuilding(player);
        }

        private GameObject FindPlayerInRange()
        {
            var candidates = GameObject.FindGameObjectsWithTag(playerTag);
            Vector3 origin = entryPoint != null ? entryPoint.position : transform.position;

            foreach (var candidate in candidates)
            {
                if (Vector3.Distance(candidate.transform.position, origin) <= interactRadius)
                {
                    return candidate;
                }
            }

            return null;
        }

        public void EnterBuilding(GameObject player)
        {
            if (player == null || _transitioning)
            {
                return;
            }

            _cachedPlayer = player;
            _transitioning = true;

            if (loadInteriorScene && !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(interiorSceneName))
            {
                SceneManager.sceneLoaded += OnInteriorSceneLoaded;
                SceneManager.LoadScene(interiorSceneName, LoadSceneMode.Single);
                return;
            }

            ActivateInteriorAndMovePlayer();
        }

        private void OnInteriorSceneLoaded(Scene scene, LoadSceneMode mode)
        {
            SceneManager.sceneLoaded -= OnInteriorSceneLoaded;
            ActivateInteriorAndMovePlayer();
        }

        private void ActivateInteriorAndMovePlayer()
        {
            if (interiorRoot != null)
            {
                interiorRoot.SetActive(true);
            }

            if (_cachedPlayer != null && interiorSpawnPoint != null)
            {
                MovePlayerToSpawn(_cachedPlayer, interiorSpawnPoint);
            }

            if (hideExteriorOnEnter)
            {
                SetExteriorVisibility(false);
            }

            _transitioning = false;
        }

        private void MovePlayerToSpawn(GameObject player, Transform spawn)
        {
            if (playerCharacterController == null)
            {
                playerCharacterController = player.GetComponent<CharacterController>();
            }

            if (playerCharacterController != null)
            {
                playerCharacterController.enabled = false;
            }

            player.transform.SetPositionAndRotation(spawn.position, spawn.rotation);

            if (playerCharacterController != null)
            {
                playerCharacterController.enabled = true;
            }
        }

        private void SetExteriorVisibility(bool visible)
        {
            var renderers = GetComponentsInChildren<Renderer>(true);
            foreach (var renderer in renderers)
            {
                renderer.enabled = visible;
            }
        }

        private void OnDrawGizmosSelected()
        {
            Vector3 origin = entryPoint != null ? entryPoint.position : transform.position;
            Gizmos.color = Color.green;
            Gizmos.DrawWireSphere(origin, interactRadius);
        }
    }
}

```
